msg:Century Golden Source is an old brand. This store opened in 2010. At that time, it should be a relatively good hotel in Hefei. I chose this place when I came back to visit relatives and go on business trips. I stayed here for 6 days and took my elderly parents to experience it. The elderly are more accustomed to this style of hotel.

Facilities: The decoration is relatively old, it is a classic style of the millennium, retro style, old-fashioned five-star, the TV is not smart, the bedding is OK, and the pillows are good. The bathroom is separated into three sections and is quite spacious. The bathtub has two types: sunken and separate. The bathtubs are different in several rooms. The bedroom space is relatively large, which is one of the reasons for choosing here. The takeaway cannot be delivered, and there is no robot delivery. All the necessary configurations are available, which is enough.

The banquet hall on the second floor is online, and basically I have to come here for family banquets every year.

Environment: Overall, it is good, the sound insulation is OK, and the floor I booked is relatively high, so it is not noisy outside. The breakfast dining area is large, the time is reasonable, and there are many types of food, but the taste is general, nothing special, and it is more traditional.
Not many people use the gym, it's underground.

Service: Young girls provide better service, the girls at the front desk have a good service attitude, including the banquet hall. Young practitioners provide much better service than middle-aged and older practitioners.

The cleaning auntie is a matter of luck. The auntie who worked two days after check-in was better, but the auntie who worked two days ago came to knock on the door very early, and she still knocked on the door even after I hit Do Not Disturb. (But when I set the "please clean" function, she didn't clean again... I went out at 10 o'clock in the morning and came back at 9 o'clock in the evening, and no one cleaned the room). Another time, someone was still in the room, and the auntie came in. I said I just needed to help change the water, but she was still walking around the room, doing this and that, and the freezer was not replenished in time. It seems that employee training should focus on the room cleaning depar**ent (toiletries were not replenished in time). The auntie in the banquet hall also kept interrupting others and kept asking if they wanted to change the bone dish.

The price is 4-500, which is okay.

But for friends who have rich experience in hotels and have requirements for experience, I would like to share my personal weekend travel experience as follows: 1. Old hotel, you know the interior and taste; 2. The hotel specializes in conferences and marriages, and the conference occupancy standard is only 350, so you Breakfast at regular prices can only be based on group meal standards. The small amount of desserts provided for breakfast should be compared to 3-star standards. In addition, the disposable items provided were of low quality, and the slippers smelled of glue, so I threw them out when I went to bed at night; 3. A large parking space in the hotel square was roped up and not parked. I don‚Äôt know what the operation was, but it took me a long time to find a parking space. Stopped far away; 4. If you want to go swimming for leisure, be mentally prepared: the water temperature of the swimming pool is low, and it is not recommended for those who do not exercise often. It may be mainly for locals to swim, the locker room is quite dirty, and there are many shoe marks on the stools. I rushed you up at 8:45 in the evening (marked to end at 9:00). When we were swimming and bathing, the employees rushed to get off work to clean up, and dirty water poured into the bathroom where we were taking a bath! The swimming pool is closed the next morning, so you can basically only experience the water for half an hour after a full meal on the night you check in; 5. The hotel's promotional page has billiards and table tennis, but they are charged for guests! I can't afford it, and this is the first time I've encountered this; 6. Children who are over 1.2 meters tall are charged for breakfast, and the policy is enforced effectively. If my height is more than a few centimeters, I have no problem with being charged, but if you charge it, it will not be included in the room rate, and it will be charged separately. It would be strange to issue a meal ticket. I saw many children going to play ice cream, and my son also went there. When he went, the waiter came up and said no, and told me to remember to sign and pay the breakfast fee, feeling that I would default on the bill; 7. The floor is high, The elevators are open less frequently, and the waiting time for the elevators is long. The windows are closed. As other reviews have mentioned, the high-rise buildings also avoid enjoying the city view. 8. When issuing check-out tickets, should I take the initiative to put it in an envelope? However, if there is no, should I take the initiative? Ask customers if they have parked their cars, instead of asking them to come back to you in the rain to solve the problem of parking and going out? 9. It is too far from the Hefei tourist check-in point, 40 minutes by car. Alas, I really don‚Äôt know why I checked out of the International Hotel by Chaohu Lake for one night and chose this hotel. The points mentioned above are completely opposite. I regret it, forget it. Will not come again! ! ! Perhaps consumers cannot have too high expectations and requirements for merchants. Personal experience, for reference only.
